### [1] [Twisting BFSS & IKKT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22318)
*Fabian Hahner,Natalie M. Paquette*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究BFSS矩阵量子力学和IKKT矩阵模型在N→∞极限下的"扭曲全息"对偶性，计算BV-BRST形式下的上同调，并与IIA/IIB弦理论的对应扭曲建立联系


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究矩阵模型与弦理论/超引力之间的全息对偶关系，通过扭曲理论揭示隐藏的无穷维对称代数，为理解M-理论与弦理论的深层联系提供新视角

Method: 使用BV-BRST形式体系识别矩阵模型的容许扭曲，计算其同调，在平面极限和微扰理论中与弦理论的对应扭曲建立映射，并分析超引力扭曲的零模截断

Result: 成功识别了BFSS和IKKT模型的扭曲，建立了它们与IIA和IIB弦理论扭曲的对应关系，揭示了扭曲引力对偶中显现的无穷维对称代数，并发现BFSS对偶的IIA超引力扭曲可作为11维超引力最小和最大扭曲的零模截断

Conclusion: 扭曲全息方法为研究矩阵模型与弦理论/超引力的对偶性提供了新框架，揭示了隐藏的对称性结构，并为理解M-理论与弦理论的深层联系开辟了新途径

Abstract: In this note we initiate the study of ``twisted holography'' for the dualities involving the BFSS matrix quantum mechanics and the IKKT matrix model in their $N \rightarrow \infty$ limits. We identify the admissible twists of each model, compute their cohomology in the BV-BRST formalism, and identify them -- in the planar limit and in perturbation theory around the trivial background -- with corresponding twists of IIA and IIB string theories, respectively. The twisted gravitational duals make manifest certain infinite dimensional symmetry algebras. In the BFSS example, the dual IIA supergravity twists are also obtained as certain zero mode truncations of the minimal (1/16-BPS) and maximal (1/4-BPS) twists of eleven-dimensional supergravity.

</details>


### [2] [Resurgence in the Virasoro Minimal String and 3d Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22335)
*Maximilian Schwick*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文使用厄米矩阵模型技术计算了Virasoro最小弦和3d引力的非微扰、复兴贡献，发现了负张力D膜、复兴壁交叉现象，并将这些结果与3d引力中的黑洞行为联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Virasoro最小弦和3d引力的非微扰效应，理解D膜物理、复兴现象与引力理论之间的深层联系，特别是黑洞行为的非微扰起源。

Method: 使用厄米矩阵模型技术，通过Zak变换构造完全非微扰的配分函数，分析负张力D膜（对应矩阵模型中的反本征值），研究复兴壁交叉现象，并应用复兴大阶渐近分析进行验证。

Result: 构造了Virasoro最小弦的完全非微扰配分函数；发现了负张力D膜与矩阵模型中反本征值的对应关系；观察到ZZ-和FZZT-膜之间的复兴壁交叉现象；在3d引力中发现了双指数型的非微扰贡献；识别了本征值密度边缘的Stokes转变与黑洞行为的关联。

Conclusion: 厄米矩阵模型为研究弦论和引力理论的非微扰结构提供了有力框架，揭示了D膜物理、复兴现象与引力效应（特别是黑洞行为）之间的深刻联系，为理解量子引力的非微扰性质开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We compute non-perturbative, resurgent contributions to the Virasoro minimal string and 3d gravity using techniques from hermitian matrix models. In particular, we construct a fully non-perturbative partition function for the Virasoro minimal string in terms of a Zak transform. In this context, negative tension D-branes appear naturally, which in the matrix model correspond to anti-eigenvalues, or instantons on the involuted sheet of the spectral curve. We further extend this analysis to resolvents and observe resurgent wall crossing phenomena between ZZ- and FZZT-branes. Using recent results that relate the Virasoro minimal string to 3d gravity with end-of-the-world branes we proceed to study the resurgent consequences of summing over the genus in 3d gravity, where we find non-perturbative contributions of doubly exponential type. These statements are then tested using resurgent large-order asymptotics. Lastly, we compute the non-perturbative eigenvalue density for generic hermitian matrix models and identify the change of asymptotic behavior at the edge of the eigenvalue distribution with a Stokes transition. This allows us to identify oscillations in the eigenvalue density with anti-Stokes behavior of FZZT-branes. In the case of 3d gravity with end-of-the-world branes we comment how this Stokes transition coincides with the onset of black hole behaviour and compute the non-perturbative primary density. Furthermore, we apply these techniques to the eigenvalue density of JT gravity to compute higher genus corrections.

</details>


### [3] [Strings on freely acting orbifolds: Spectra, moduli spaces and branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22354)
*George Gkountoumis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究IIB型弦理论在自由作用轨道折叠上的紧致化，特别关注非几何弦紧致化的非对称轨道折叠，使用对偶扭曲和格点两种方法，探讨超对称保持、模空间、沼泽地猜想验证及D-膜谱系等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自由作用轨道折叠（特别是非对称轨道折叠）作为非几何弦紧致化的代表，探索弦景观中的特殊角落。这些构造提供了研究超对称破缺、模空间几何、量子修正以及验证沼泽地猜想等基本问题的理想框架。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：对偶扭曲方法和格点方法。首先构建自由作用（非对称）轨道折叠的一般构造，重点关注闭弦部分。通过具体例子展示五维中保持N=6,4,2或0超对称的轨道折叠，并将轨道折叠与Scherk-Schwarz约化联系起来。研究模空间特殊点处的质量谱变化，分析非超对称轨道折叠的稳定性条件。

Result: 1. 建立了自由作用轨道折叠与Scherk-Schwarz约化的对应关系，通过匹配最轻的非扭曲轨道折叠态与有效超引力理论态。2. 发现在模空间特殊点处，通常有质量的扭曲态可以变得无质量。3. 证明非超对称轨道折叠在远离模空间特殊区域时可以无快子。4. 确定了五维N=2超对称轨道折叠的经典超多重态和矢量多重态模空间。5. 通过构造对偶轨道折叠对，论证矢量多重态模空间度量无量子修正。6. 验证了沼泽地距离猜想在研究的非几何紧致化中成立。7. 确定了各种D-膜在轨道折叠下存活的条件。

Conclusion: 该论文系统研究了IIB型弦理论在自由作用轨道折叠上的紧致化，特别是非对称轨道折叠作为非几何紧致化的性质。研究揭示了轨道折叠构造与Scherk-Schwarz约化的深刻联系，证明了非超对称构造的稳定性，确定了模空间结构并验证了沼泽地猜想，为理解弦景观中的非几何紧致化提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In this dissertation, we study various aspects of type IIB string theory compactified on freely acting orbifolds. We focus particularly on asymmetric orbifolds, which are examples of non-geometric string compactifications and constitute an intriguing corner in the string landscape. We describe the orbifolds using two complementary approaches; the duality twists and the lattice approach. First, we discuss the general construction of freely acting (asymmetric) orbifolds, focusing on the closed string sector. Afterwards, we present explicit examples of orbifolds preserving $\mathcal{N} = 6,4,2$ or $0$ supersymmetry in five dimensions and we demonstrate the connection between freely acting orbifolds and Scherk-Schwarz reductions by matching the lightest untwisted orbifold states with those arising form the effective supergravity theory. Regarding the orbifold twisted sectors, we show that at special points in the moduli space, generically massive states can become massless. Furthermore, we show that the spectrum of non-supersymmetric orbifolds can become tachyon-free away from special loci in the moduli space. Next, we turn our attention to the orbifold moduli space, and we focus on orbifolds preserving $\mathcal{N} = 2$ supersymmetry in five dimensions, for which we determine the classical hypermultiplet and vector multiplet moduli spaces. Moreover, by constructing dual orbifold pairs, we argue that no quantum corrections to the metric on the vector multiplet moduli space arise. Then, we discuss aspects of the swampland program in the context of freely acting asymmetric orbifolds and we verify that the swampland distance conjecture is valid in the non-geometric compactifications of string theory studied in this thesis. Finally, we focus on the D-brane spectrum of freely acting orbifolds and we determine the conditions under which the various D-branes survive the orbifolding.

</details>


### [4] [Modified Euler-Heisenberg effective action and Proper-Time Method in Lorentz-Violating Scalar QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2405.20855)
*L. C. T. Brito,J. C. C. Felipe,A. C. Lehum,J. R. Nascimento,A. Yu. Petrov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在洛伦兹破缺的标量量子电动力学框架下，计算了单圈欧拉-海森堡型有效作用量，研究了真空中的量子光子效应，评估了可能影响光子-光子散射的非线性洛伦兹破缺贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究真空中的量子光子效应，为测试量子电动力学和超越标准模型的物理提供预测源。特别关注洛伦兹破缺对量子电动力学的影响。

Method: 在洛伦兹破缺的标量量子电动力学框架下，计算了单圈欧拉-海森堡型有效作用量。考虑了CPT偶和CPT奇两种情况，获得了应力张量F_{μν}所有阶的精确结果，并显式评估了该有效作用量的低阶项。

Result: 以显式规范不变的方式识别了来自洛伦兹破缺的量子效应。显式评估了可能影响光子-光子散射的非线性洛伦兹破缺贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究为在洛伦兹破缺背景下理解量子电动力学效应提供了理论框架，特别关注了光子-光子散射等非线性效应，为测试超越标准模型的物理提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Quantum photon effects in vacuum provide an interesting setting to test quantum electrodynamics, serving as a source for predictions about physics beyond the Standard Model. In this paper, we investigate these effects by calculating the one-loop Euler-Heisenberg-like effective action within a Lorentz-violating scalar quantum electrodynamics framework. In both CPT-even and CPT-odd scenarios, we obtain the exact result in all orders of the stress tensor $F_{μν}$ and evaluate explicitly the lower orders of this effective action. We identify the quantum effects coming from Lorentz violation in an explicitly gauge invariant way. Nonlinear Lorentz-violating contributions that may affect photon-photon scattering are explicitly evaluated.

</details>


### [5] [Continuous symmetries and charge measurement of boundary operators in holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22377)
*Ibrahima Bah,Federico Bonetti,Mufaro Chitoto,Enoch Leung*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究全息电荷测量：通过边界悬挂的U形缺陷测量连续内对称性的电荷，建立场论与全息对偶的对应关系


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究全息对偶中连续内对称性的电荷测量问题，探索边界算符与体规范场之间的对应关系，理解场论中连续对称性算符的厚化正则化在全息框架下的实现

Method: 1. 从低能角度推导电荷测量过程的普适特征；2. 使用边界悬挂的U形缺陷进行电荷测量；3. 在Type IIB弦理论和M理论中提供具体的AdS/CFT实现；4. 分析Type IIB构造中的膜动力学；5. 研究悬挂膜构型的拓扑性质及其融合规则

Result: 1. 建立了边界带电算符与体规范场Wilson线之间的对应关系；2. 展示了悬挂缺陷图像如何模拟场论中连续对称性算符的厚化正则化；3. 实现了阿贝尔和非阿贝尔对称性的具体构造；4. 揭示了电荷测量过程中的膜动力学机制；5. 证明了悬挂膜构型的拓扑性质，并通过快子动力学解释了其融合规则

Conclusion: 该研究为全息对偶中连续内对称性的电荷测量提供了系统框架，建立了场论正则化与全息实现之间的对应关系，深化了对边界-体对应和对称性实现的理解，为研究更复杂的对称性结构奠定了基础

Abstract: We study holographic charge measurement for continuous internal symmetries. Charged boundary operators are characterized by Wilson lines of bulk gauge fields ending on the boundary, while charge measurement is performed using U-shaped defects hanging from the boundary. We derive universal features of this process from a low-energy point of view, and show how the hanging defect picture mimics the thickening regularization of continuous symmetry operators in field theory. Furthermore, we provide explicit top-down realizations in AdS/CFT setups in Type IIB string theory and M-theory, featuring Abelian as well as non-Abelian symmetries. In the case of Type IIB constructions, we analyze the brane dynamics underlying the charge measurement process. Along the way, we also characterize how hanging brane configurations can be regarded as being topological, and demonstrate how tachyon dynamics account for their fusion rules.

</details>


### [6] [Self-Dual Gauge Fields from Superstring Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22420)
*Chris Hull*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文从新构建的超弦场理论中推导出了自对偶规范场的作用量，该作用量在特定极限下简化为Sen的作用量，描述了两个解耦的自对偶规范场分别耦合到两个不同的度规上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从新构建的超弦场理论出发，推导自对偶规范场的作用量，探索超弦场理论与自对偶规范场理论之间的联系，并研究在特定极限下如何还原到已知的Sen理论。

Method: 基于新构建的超弦场理论，通过特定极限过程推导出自对偶规范场的作用量。分析该作用量的结构，包括两个解耦的自对偶规范场分别耦合到两个不同度规的特性，以及背景度规的存在。

Result: 成功从超弦场理论推导出自对偶规范场的新作用量，该作用量在特定极限下简化为Sen的作用量。发现该理论描述了两个解耦的自对偶规范场，每个场只耦合到一个度规，总共涉及三个度规（两个耦合度规和一个背景度规）。作用量具有两个自旋-2规范不变性，微分同胚来自对角子群。

Conclusion: 新构建的超弦场理论为自对偶规范场提供了新的作用量形式，揭示了超弦理论与自对偶规范场之间的深刻联系。该作用量具有独特的三个度规耦合结构，为理解弦理论中的规范场动力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: The action for self-dual gauge fields that emerges from the recently constructed superstring field theory is found. The new superstring field theory reduces to that of Sen in a certain limit, and in this limit the new action for self-dual gauge fields reduces to Sen's action for such fields. The theory describes two decoupled self-dual gauge fields that couple to two metrics, with each gauge field coupling to only one of the metrics. The action also features a background metric, and the non-linear coupling to these three metrics is non-standard. There are two spin-two gauge invariances, and diffeomorphisms arise from the diagonal subgroup.

</details>


### [7] [Three-Dimensional Modified Klein--Gordon Oscillator in Standard and Generalized Doubly Special Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22444)
*Abdelmalek Boumali,Nosratollah Jafari*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在三维克莱因-戈登振荡器中研究双狭义相对论效应，获得解析谱和普朗克抑制偏移，为不同DSR方案提供直接比较框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双狭义相对论在光速不变之外引入第二个观测者无关尺度（普朗克尺度），在有效波动方程中表现为变形色散关系和能量依赖的空间算符。本文旨在量化这些效应在典型可解束缚态问题中的表现。

Method: 研究三维克莱因-戈登振荡器，分析两种标准DSR实现（Amelino-Camelia和Magueijo-Smolin）以及基于普朗克长度一阶展开的广义DSR框架。通过定态约化和球坐标分离，保持未变形振荡器的广义拉盖尔函数和球谐函数结构，DSR仅变形代数量子化条件。

Result: 标准DSR情况获得闭式谱，广义模型获得微扰普朗克抑制偏移。所有实现中变形都引起正负能量解的分支依赖偏移，偏移随激发增加而增大，在k→∞或l_p→0时平滑消失。

Conclusion: 成功提取解析谱和普朗克抑制偏移，为不同DSR方案在完全三维设置中的直接比较提供了基础，展示了DSR变形在束缚态问题中的具体量化效应。

Abstract: Doubly Special Relativity (DSR) augments special relativity by introducing, alongside the invariant speed of light $c$, a second observer-independent scale typically associated with the Planck regime. At the level of effective wave equations this principle manifests itself through deformed dispersion relations and energy-dependent spatial operators. Here we quantify such effects in a prototypical exactly solvable bound-state problem: the three-dimensional Klein--Gordon oscillator generated by a non-minimal momentum coupling that yields isotropic harmonic confinement while preserving rotational symmetry. We analyze two standard DSR realizations (Amelino--Camelia and Magueijo--Smolin, parametrized by an invariant energy scale $k$) as well as a generalized DSR framework based on a first-order expansion in the Planck length $l_p$. After stationary reduction and separation in spherical coordinates, the eigenfunctions retain the generalized-Laguerre and spherical-harmonic structure of the undeformed oscillator, whereas DSR deforms the algebraic quantization condition that relates the principal oscillator number $N=2n+\ell\in\mathbb{N}_0$ to the relativistic energy. Closed-form spectra are obtained for the standard DSR cases, and perturbative Planck-suppressed shifts are derived for the generalized model. In all realizations the deformation induces branch-dependent shifts of both positive- and negative-energy solutions, which increase with excitation and vanish smoothly in the limits $k\to\infty$ or $l_p\to0$. The main goal of this paper is to extract analytic spectra and Planck-suppressed shifts that enable a direct comparison between different DSR prescriptions in a fully three-dimensional setting.

</details>


### [8] [Higher dualities in E11 exceptional field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22491)
*Guillaume Bossard,Nicolas Boulanger,Josh O'Connor*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在E11例外场论的线性化层面，证明了存在E11不变性的十一维超引力公式化猜想，其中传播场通过无限塔的高阶对偶实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证关于E11不变性十一维超引力公式化的猜想，该理论中传播场通过无限塔的高阶对偶场实现。

Method: 在E11例外场论的线性化层面，从伪拉格朗日量出发，为与三形式、六形式和对偶引力子相关的所有高阶梯度对偶场构造父作用量。

Result: 证明了欧拉-拉格朗日方程约束Stueckelberg场为纯旋度，确保高阶对偶传播与原始超引力场相同的物理自由度；额外的Stueckelberg场作为高阶对偶场Labastida张量的源发挥特定作用。

Conclusion: 在E11例外场论的线性化层面明确证明了E11不变性十一维超引力公式化的猜想，阐明了高阶对偶场的物理实现机制。

Abstract: It has been conjectured that there exists an E11-invariant formulation of eleven-dimensional supergravity in which the propagating fields of the theory are realised through an infinite tower of higher duals. In this work, we prove this conjecture explicitly within E11 exceptional field theory at the linearised level. Starting from the pseudo-Lagrangian, we construct parent actions for all higher gradient dual fields that are associated with the three-form, the six-form, and the dual graviton. We show that the resulting Euler-Lagrange equations constrain the Stueckelberg fields to be pure curls, ensuring that the higher duals propagate the same physical degrees of freedom as the original supergravity fields. The additional Stueckelberg fields, which are not predicted by the tensor hierarchy algebra, are shown to play a specific role as sources for the Labastida tensors of the higher dual fields.

</details>


### [9] [A Perfectoid Duality Between M-Theory and F-Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22503)
*Arshid Shabir,Bobby Eka Gunara,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非奇异的、定义层面的F理论表述，通过用完美胚几何和凝聚数学描述的塔完备化圆环取代传统的M理论收缩纤维极限，为模数据提供了内在的十一维载体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统F理论依赖于M理论中椭圆纤维收缩的奇异极限，这导致了定义层面的不完善。本文旨在为F理论提供一个非奇异的、内在的数学基础，避免传统方法中的奇异性问题。

Method: 使用完美胚几何和凝聚数学构造塔完备化圆环，取代传统的收缩纤维极限。通过规范倾斜和比较程序，将椭圆几何作为输出而非输入。在常数耦合扇区建立精确的M理论/IIB型弦论字典，并在十维玻色有效作用量层面测试对应关系。

Result: 建立了物理轴-伸缩子由十一维几何和拓扑数据固定的精确对应关系。塔完备化几何自然地组织了广义上同调中的全局扇区，电荷数据由K理论控制并展现规范的素数幂挠结构。框架可扩展到变耦合背景、对偶缺陷，并允许自然的阿代尔完备化。

Conclusion: 该框架为F理论及其扩展提供了一个连贯的、非奇异的基础，统一了模数据、全局扇区、拓扑耦合和对偶对称性，为弦论和M理论的数学基础提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We present a non-singular, definition-level formulation of F-theory by replacing the traditional shrinking-fiber limit of M-theory with compactification on a tower-completed circle described using perfectoid geometry and condensed mathematics. This construction provides an intrinsic eleven-dimensional carrier for modular data and admits a canonical tilting and comparison procedure that yields elliptic geometry as an output rather than an auxiliary input. Using this framework, we establish a precise M-theory/Type IIB dictionary in the constant-coupling sector, showing how the physical axio-dilaton is fixed by eleven-dimensional geometric and topological data. The correspondence is tested at the level of the ten-dimensional bosonic effective action, including its topological couplings inherited from eleven dimensions. The tower-completed geometry naturally organizes global sectors in generalized cohomology, with charge data governed by K-theory and exhibiting a canonical prime-power torsion structure. We further show how this framework extends to varying-coupling backgrounds and duality defects, admits a natural adelic completion with prime-independence, and generalizes to higher-rank and U-duality geometries. We also discuss holographic aspects and the anomaly-refined extension of the duality group beyond the bosonic truncation. Together, these results provide a coherent, non-singular foundation for F-theory and its extensions.

</details>


### [10] [Geodesic equation in noncommutative space: a field theory perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22726)
*Carolina Matté Gregory,Tajron Jurić,Aleksandr Pinzul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过场论方法推导了Moyal型非对易时空中点粒子的测地线方程，发现所有非对易效应被吸收到一个有效的位置依赖质量函数M(x)中，导致测地线方程出现一个由时空量子性质源起的外部力项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非对易时空中粒子的运动规律，探索量子时空几何对经典测地线方程的修正，理解量子引力效应在粒子动力学中的表现。

Method: 采用场论方法，基于非对易Klein-Gordon方程的准经典极限，从扭曲几何构造的协变Laplace-Beltrami算子出发，推导非对易Hamilton-Jacobi方程，将非对易效应吸收到有效质量函数中，进而得到修正的测地线方程。

Result: 1. 所有非对易效应被吸收到有效位置依赖质量函数M(x)中，出现在标准相对论色散关系中；2. 测地线方程获得附加项，形式为固定外力F_NC^μ = -1/2 g^{μν}∂_νM^2(x)；3. 对一般度规计算了有效质量到非对易参数的四阶微扰，证明所有奇数阶修正恒为零；4. 对(r-θ)扭曲应用于球对称背景的具体情况，得到显式表达式，显示主要修正出现在Θ^2阶，与探测粒子质量成正比，而质量为零粒子不受影响。

Conclusion: 非对易时空中的粒子动力学可以通过有效位置依赖质量函数来描述，测地线方程获得由时空量子性质源起的外部力修正，这种修正对质量粒子在二阶非对易参数下出现，而质量为零粒子保持经典测地线运动。

Abstract: We derive the geodesic equation for point particles propagating in Moyal-type noncommutative spacetimes using a field-theoretic approach based on the quasi-classical limit of the noncommutative Klein-Gordon equation. Starting from a twisted-geometric construction of the covariant Laplace-Beltrami operator, we obtain the noncommutative Hamilton-Jacobi equation and show that all noncommutative effects are absorbed into an effective, position-dependent mass function $M(x)$ appearing in an otherwise standard relativistic dispersion relation. The corresponding particle dynamics then acquires an additional term in the geodesic equation that takes the form of a fixed external force $F_{\text{NC}}^μ= -\frac{1}{2} g^{μν}\partial_νM^2(x)$, sourced entirely by the quantum nature of spacetime. We compute this effective mass perturbatively up to fourth order in the noncommutativity parameter for a general metric, proving that all odd-order corrections vanish identically. For the specific case of an $(r-θ)$ twist applied to spherically symmetric backgrounds, we obtain explicit expressions demonstrating that the leading correction to geodesic motion appears at $Θ^2$ order and is proportional to the probe particle's mass, while massless particles remain unaffected.

</details>


### [11] [Magnetized BPS lumps in the $CP^1$ model with Maxwell coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22957)
*I. B. Cunha,F. C. E. Lima,Aldo Vera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究CP¹模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中的BPS拓扑构型，发现磁通量量子化，数值求解BPS方程得到正则、磁局域、能量稳定的构型，其内部结构由CP¹靶空间几何刚性控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究CP¹模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中的BPS拓扑构型，探索不同于Abelian Higgs涡旋的拓扑激发机制，后者依赖于自发对称性破缺，而前者纯粹源于CP¹靶空间的几何结构。

Method: 从非线性O(3) sigma模型出发，显式构造其到CP¹表述的经典映射，强调与Fubini-Study靶空间几何内在关联的局部U(1)规范对称性的涌现。在静态扇区分析磁化BPS lump构型，通过拓扑边界条件证明磁通量量子化。在BPS框架内识别自对偶构型存在所需的自相互作用势，详细分析lump核心附近和空间无穷远处的渐近行为。数值求解BPS方程。

Result: 磁通量量子化且完全由规范场的渐近行为决定。有限能解必然对应CP¹靶空间中的lump-like BPS构型，标量场渐近消失。数值求解BPS方程得到正则、磁局域、能量稳定的构型，其内部结构由CP¹靶空间几何刚性控制。这些构型不依赖于自发对称性破缺，纯粹源于CP¹靶空间的几何。

Conclusion: 成功构建并分析了CP¹模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中的BPS拓扑构型，揭示了不同于传统Abelian Higgs涡旋的几何起源机制。这些构型具有正则性、磁局域性和能量稳定性，其性质由CP¹靶空间的几何结构决定，为研究几何诱导的拓扑激发提供了新范例。

Abstract: We investigate Bogomolnyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) topological configurations in the $CP^1$ model minimally coupled to a Maxwell gauge field. Starting from the nonlinear $O(3)$ sigma model, we explicitly construct its classical mapping to the $CP^1$ formulation, emphasizing the emergence of a local $U(1)$ gauge symmetry intrinsically linked to the Fubini-Study target-space geometry. Focusing on the static sector, we analyze magnetized BPS lump configurations. By examining the topological boundary conditions, we show that the magnetic flux is quantized and fully determined by the asymptotic behavior of the gauge field. Within the BPS framework, we identify the specific self-interaction potential required for the existence of self-dual configurations. A detailed analysis of the asymptotic behavior, both near the lump core and at spatial infinity, demonstrates that finite-energy solutions necessarily correspond to lump-like BPS configurations in the $CP^1$ target space, with the scalar field vanishing asymptotically. The resulting BPS equations are solved numerically, and the main physical properties of the solutions are presented. We find that these configurations are regular, magnetically localized, and energetically stable, with their internal structure rigidly controlled by the geometry of the $CP^1$ target space. In contrast to Abelian Higgs vortices, the configurations discussed here do not rely on spontaneous symmetry breaking but arise purely from the geometry of the $CP^1$ target space.

### [12] [Holomorphic Quantization in Constant Curvature Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22984)
*Dmitri Bykov,Viacheslav Krivorol*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为二维常曲率黎曼背景上的自由点粒子开发一种系统性的量子化方案，统一处理平面、环面、球面和双曲平面等不同几何背景下的量子化问题

Method: 基于拉格朗日嵌入方法，将粒子构型空间嵌入背景等距群的余伴随轨道乘积中，通过全纯量子化技术处理不同几何背景（包括有/无单极场的情况）

Result: 成功推导出各种背景下的哈密顿量谱和波函数，并获得了Repka关于SL(2,R)离散级数表示张量积分解结果的几何和物理解释

Abstract: We present a holomorphic quantization scheme for free point particles on two-dimensional constant curvature Riemannian backgrounds. The procedure is based on a Lagrangian embedding of the particle configuration space into a product of coadjoint orbits of the background isometry group. Examples are provided by particles on the plane, torus, sphere, and hyperbolic plane, with or without a monopole field. We elaborate the method by recovering the Hamiltonian spectrum and the wave functions on such spaces. As a by-product, we obtain a geometric and physical interpretation of Repka's result on the decomposition of tensor products of $\mathbf{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$ discrete series representations.

### [13] [On BRST Lagrangian description of partially massless bosonic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23091)
*I. L. Buchbinder,S. A. Fedoruk,V. A. Krykhtin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了四维空间中部分无质量玻色场的完整BRST拉格朗日描述，使用(A)dS空间中的二分量自旋张量，通过将第二类约束转换为第一类约束构建厄米且幂零的BRST荷，最终在dS空间中构造规范不变拉格朗日量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究部分无质量玻色场在四维(A)dS空间中的规范理论描述，解决第二类约束的处理问题，建立完整的BRST量子化框架。

Method: 使用二分量自旋张量表述基本场，将质量壳条件重新表述为Fock空间向量约束，开发第二类约束转换为第一类约束的转换程序，构建厄米且幂零的BRST荷，基于BRST荷构造规范不变拉格朗日量。

Result: 证明了BRST荷的厄米性和幂零性限制了理论参数条件，这些条件仅在dS空间中满足，与AdS空间不兼容；构造了包含(s-t)个Stückelberg场的规范不变拉格朗日量，运动方程精确再现质量壳条件。

Conclusion: 成功建立了四维dS空间中部分无质量玻色场的完整BRST拉格朗日描述，解决了第二类约束处理问题，为这类场的规范理论提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We present an exhaustive BRST lagrangian description of partially massless bosonic fields in four-dimensional space. The basic fields are formulated in terms of two-component spin-tensors in (A)dS space where the tracelessness conditions are automatically fulfilled. The mass shell of partially massless fields is reformulated in terms of constraints on Fock space vectors including the second-class constraints. A conversion procedure for transforming second-class constraints into first-class ones is developed, allowing one to construct a Hermitian and nilpotent BRST charge in the Fock space under consideration. It is proven that the hermiticity and nilpotency restrict the conditions on the theory parameters, which are fulfilled only in dS space. The hermiticity of the BRST charge is incompatible with AdS space. The gauge invariant Lagrangian is constructed on the basis of the BRST charge, and for spin $s$ and depth $t$ the allowed states in the Lagrangian include only $(s-t)$ Stückelberg fields. Their exclusion leads to gauge transformations of degree $(s-t)$ for the physical fields. The Lagrangian equations of motion exactly reproduce the mass shell conditions. The Lagrangian in terms of conventional spin-tensor fields is also presented.

</details>

### [14] [Mimicking the earth core conditions with ultrafast laser materials interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22460)
*Mohamed Yaseen Noor,Aram Yedigaryan,Gabriel Calderon,Arshak Tsaturyan,Elena Kanchan,Jinwoo Hwang,Carmen S. Menoni,Jean-Philippe Colombier,Enam Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 飞秒激光激发非晶硅-铪多层介质，在亚表面区域形成高压硅相（斯石英、赛弗特石、黄铁矿型高密度结构），无需金刚石压砧即可在常温常压下合成超高压硅相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索飞秒激光创造极端非平衡热力学条件的能力，研究能否在无金刚石压砧的情况下合成和稳定超高压硅相，这对激光损伤机制、高能量密度材料和行星物理学有重要意义。

Method: 使用飞秒激光激发非晶硅-铪多层介质，通过透射电子显微镜(TEM)、选区电子衍射(SAED)和四维扫描透射电子显微镜(4D-STEM)直接映射纳米尺度相演化，结合分子动力学模拟揭示热力学转变路径。

Result: 成功合成了斯石英、赛弗特石和黄铁矿型高密度结构等高压硅相，这些相被限制在激光产生的气泡内部。分子动力学模拟揭示了快速电子压力驱动的致密化和八面体配位，随后是温度驱动的结晶和超快淬火过程中的位移相变。

Conclusion: 飞秒激光激发是一种可行的途径，可在常温常压下无需金刚石压砧合成和稳定超高压硅相，展示了双阶段转变路径，对激光损伤机制、高能量密度材料和行星物理学有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Ultrafast lasers create extreme, non-equilibrium thermodynamic conditions that can transiently reach pressures and temperatures comparable to interior core of the earth. Here we show that femtosecond excitation of amorphous silica-hafnia multilayer dielectrics drives the formation of high-pressure crystalline phases of silica including stishovite, seifertite, and the pyrite-type high density structure, within confined subsurface regions.Using TEM, SAED, and 4D-STEM, we directly map nanoscale phase evolution and identify crystalline motifs embedded inside laser generated blisters.Complementary molecular dynamics simualtions reveal the thermodynamic pathway underlying these transformations, where rapid electronic pressure initiates densification and octahedral coordination, followed by temperature driven crystallization and displacive transitions during ultrafast quenching. The resulting polymorphs reflects a dual-stage pathway inaccessible under equilibrium processing. Our results establish femtosecond laser excitation as a viable route to synthesize and stabilize ultrahigh-density high pressure silica phases under ambient conditions, without a diamond anvil cell, with implications for laser-damage mechanisms, high-energy-density materials, and planetary physics.

</details>


### [15] [The Surface Sensitivity of X-ray Second Harmonic Generation as a Function of Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22497)
*Daniel Schacher,Tod A. Pascal,Keith V. Lawler,Craig P. Schwartz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论和计算分析金刚石在X射线区域的二次谐波产生（SHG）的表面敏感性和探测深度，发现能量高于C K边（~285 eV）时SHG主要由体相四极响应主导，而近K边时具有显著表面敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究金刚石在X射线区域二次谐波产生的表面敏感性和探测深度，理解不同能量下SHG信号来源（表面vs体相）的变化规律，以及晶体取向对表面敏感性的影响。

Method: 采用速度规范实时含时密度泛函理论（VG-RT-TDDFT）进行解析和计算分析，包含完整多极展开。通过两种方法：1）计算改变可产生SHG的层数和位置；2）利用晶体对称性分析。

Result: 1）在1000 eV（远高于C K边~285 eV）时，金刚石SHG主要由体相四极响应主导；2）体相响应随能量增加而增强，到7000 eV时占绝对主导；3）近C K边时测量具有显著表面敏感性，但随能量增加而降低；4）晶体取向（如(001)和(111)终止面）对表面敏感性有显著影响。

Conclusion: 金刚石X射线区域SHG的表面敏感性强烈依赖于光子能量：近C K边时表面敏感，而高于1000 eV时主要由体相响应主导。晶体取向是影响表面敏感性的重要因素，为利用SHG进行材料表征提供了重要指导。

Abstract: The surface sensitivity and probe depth in the x-ray regime of diamond for second harmonic generation (SHG) was investigated both analytically and computationally with velocity gauge real-time time-dependent density functional theory (VG-RT-TDDFT), which includes a full multipole expansion. This was accomplished using two different approaches, by changing the number and location of layers that can generate SHG computationally and by exploiting the symmetry of a crystal, a similar pattern emerged. We find that by 1000 eV, well above the ~285 eV of the C $K$-edge, the SHG of diamond is dominated by the bulk, quadrupole response, in agreement with our analytic calculations. The bulk response continues to grow as the energy is increased, becoming overwhelming by 7000 eV. Near the C $K$-edge the measurement is quite surface sensitive, however, this surface sensitivity reduces as the energy increases such that by 1000 eV (and certainly by 3500 eV) SHG is largely bulk sensitive. Moreover, we find that the specific details of the crystal orientation (i.e., comparing a (001)-terminated and (111)-terminated surface) appear to have significant effects on the surface sensitivity.

</details>


### [16] [LLM-driven discovery for carbon allotropes with bond-network entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22706)
*Yuzhou Hao,Yujie Liu,Xuejie Li,Turab Lookman,Xiangdong Ding,Jun Sun,Zhibin Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 开发闭环AI框架结合大语言模型和机器学习势能，发现多种新型碳同素异形体，包括具有极端热各向异性、超低剪切刚度、金属导电性、负泊松比和超硬特性的碳相

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳同素异形体在热管理和机械性能方面具有重要应用价值，但传统第一性原理计算难以探索其巨大的构型空间。碳的丰富拓扑景观中sp、sp²和sp³杂化态的竞争决定了材料性能，需要新方法来高效探索这一复杂空间

Method: 建立闭环AI框架：1) 引入杂化熵描述符指导搜索；2) 使用大语言模型(CrystaLLM)生成候选结构；3) 采用迭代优化的机器学习势能进行高通量筛选和高保真验证；4) 筛选数千个结构识别稳定相

Result: 发现多种稳定碳同素异形体：1) yne-diamond C₁₂和yne-hex-diamond C₈：具有极端热各向异性和超低面内剪切刚度（sp-sp³混合杂化）；2) sp-sp²-sp³混合杂化C₁₂相：兼具金属导电性和反常负泊松比；3) 超硬相C16_3：计算维氏硬度103.3 GPa超过金刚石(96 GPa)；微观分析表明热输运由刚性框架和柔性连接体的相互作用决定

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了已知碳相空间，证明了生成式AI与机器学习势能耦合在功能材料逆向设计中的有效性，为探索复杂构型空间和发现具有定制性能的新材料提供了高效框架

Abstract: The discovery of novel carbon allotropes with tailored thermal and mechanical properties is critical for advanced thermal management. However, exploring the vast configurational space of carbon using \textit{ab initio} calculations remains computationally prohibitive. Driven by the rich topological landscape of carbon, where the competition between $sp, sp^2,$ and $sp^3$ hybridization states dictates material performance, we establish a closed-loop AI framework to explore this complex configurational space. We introduce a hybridization entropy descriptor to guide the search beyond conventional forms. Here, we establish a closed-loop AI framework that synergizes a Large Language Model (LLM) for structural generation with a Machine Learning Potential (MLP) for accelerated evaluation. Leveraging CrystaLLM to generate candidates and an iteratively refined MLP for high-fidelity validation, we screened thousands of structures to identify several stable allotropes with exotic properties. Specifically, we report ``yne-diamond C$_{12}$'' and ``yne-hex-diamond C$_{8}$'', which exhibit extreme thermal anisotropy and ultralow in-plane shear stiffness arising from their mixed $sp$-$sp^3$ hybridization. Furthermore, we discovered a complex $sp$-$sp^2$-$sp^3$ hybridized C$_{12}$ phase that combines metallic conductivity with an anomalous negative Poisson's ratio. Notably, we identified a superhard phase (C16_3) possessing a calculated Vickers hardness (103.3 GPa) exceeding that of diamond 96 GPa). Microscopic analysis reveals that thermal transport in these materials is governed by the interplay between rigid frameworks and flexible linkers. This work expands the known carbon phase space and demonstrates the efficacy of coupling generative AI with machine learning potentials for the accelerated inverse design of functional materials.

</details>


### [17] [Role of the Nephelauxetic Effect in Engineering Mn4+ Luminescence Kinetics for Lifetime-Based Thermometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22728)
*A. Basheer,M. Szymczak,M. Piasecki,A. M. Srivastava,M. G. Brik,L. Marciniak*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于发射动力学的发光测温技术潜力巨大，但用于有意预测测温性能的可靠工具仍然有限。当前工作旨在解决这一挑战，通过理论描述Mn4+离子的2E态寿命和灵敏度来开发预测模型。

Method: 引入了一种基于双钙钛矿体系（Sr2InNbO6、Sr2InTaO6、Ba2InTaO6、Ba2InNbO6）中Mn4+离子的方法，通过红移效应（nephelauxetic effect）理论描述2E态寿命、绝对灵敏度和相对灵敏度。重点分析了β1参数而非传统的Dq/B比。

Result: 研究结果表明，与常见假设相反，Dq/B比不是Mn4+离子光谱行为或Mn4+掺杂荧光粉测温性能的主要影响因素。相反，红移效应β1参数起主导作用。经验分析开发了一个预测模型，能够仅基于β1参数估算SAMAX和SRMAX值。

Conclusion: 该方法代表了向理性设计具有预定测温特性的基于寿命的发光温度计迈出的重要一步，可根据特定应用需求定制测温性能。

Abstract: Although the considerable potential of luminescence thermometry based on emission kinetics has been widely demonstrated, reliable tools for the intentional prediction of thermometric performance remain limited. To address this challenge, the present work introduces an approach that enables a theoretical description of the 2E state lifetime of Mn4+ ions, as well as the absolute and relative sensitivities, in terms of the nephelauxetic effect within the group of double perovskites: Sr2InNbO6, Sr2InTaO6, Ba2InTaO6, and Ba2InNbO6. Our results clearly show that, contrary to common assumptions, the Dq/B ratio is not the primary factor governing either the spectroscopic behavior of Mn4+ ions or the thermometric performance of Mn4+-doped phosphors. Instead, the nephelauxetic beta1 parameter plays the dominant role. The empirical analysis carried out in this study led to the development of a predictive model that enables estimation of SAMAX and SRMAX values based exclusively on beta1. This methodology represents a significant step toward the rational design of lifetime-based luminescence thermometers with predefined thermometric characteristics tailored to the requirements of specific applications.

Abstract: Thermal quenching (TQ) generally occurs in phosphors and is ascribed to the activation of non-radiative transitions at elevated temperatures. This effect limits the use of most phosphors in high-power/high-temperature applications, such as outdoor lighting and laser systems. To achieve anti-TQ properties, structural design of phosphors is required. This usually follows two guidelines: (1) increasing lattice rigidity to minimize thermal expansion; (2) converting thermal energy into radiative transitions to compensate for the non-radiative losses. While metal oxides and metal nitrides dominate the field of commercial anti-TQ phosphors, metal halides - despite their inherently soft lattices - have shown remarkable progress as anti-TQ phosphors in recent years. Here, we review the advances in anti-TQ metal halides (covering the time span from 2017, when first reports have appeared, till today) and discuss their mechanisms and applications. We argue that the low synthesis temperatures of metal halides and their high photoluminescence quantum yields (PLQYs) make them promising candidates as anti-TQ phosphors. Furthermore, since the rich optical-physical processes underlying the anti-TQ effect in soft-lattice in metal halides are only now beginning to be unraveled, this creates opportunities for many fundamental investigations.

Abstract: H2-H2O redox cycling of iron powder beds at 650-800 °C offers a compact, safe, economical hydrogen storage method, but sintering-induced capacity loss has stalled its scalability for decades. Here, we show that adding redox-active tungsten to Fe powders solves this problem in static powder beds: Fe-25W (at%) alloyed powder self-foams during redox cycling via W gas-phase transport, increasing porosity and preserving capacity. In a custom automated reactor, a kilogram-scale powder bed reversibly stores 42g H2 and sustains 96+/-3% capacity utilization over 30 redox cycles. Temperature-resolved in-situ X-ray diffraction reveals a chemical-vapor-transport-mediated self-foaming mechanism that redistributes W to refine the microstructure, complemented by a contact-barrier stabilization mechanism during high-temperature holds. Partial-capacity cycling up to 90 cycles further confirms sintering resistance under incomplete redox conditions. These results establish Fe-W powder beds as a robust, scalable, and compact platform for safe, stationary hydrogen storage.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出动态碰撞指纹（DCF）框架，通过动态探测原子结构生成简洁、物理意义明确的描述符。使用120个二维碳同素异形体数据集，与Matminer库进行性能对比。采用线性回归、决策树和XGBoost三种回归模型，在10%到90%的训练/测试划分上评估，并通过多次随机种子重复实验以表征统计变异性。

Conclusion: DCF作为结构表示方法，是高维描述符库的重要替代方案，既具有计算灵活性又具备物理基础。

Abstract: In materials science, the selection of structural descriptors for machine learning protocols strongly influences predictive performance and the degree of physical interpretability that can be achieved from the derived models. Although more complex descriptors may improve numerical accuracy, they often represent extra computational load, also reducing transparency into the underlying structural information. A framework called the Dynamic Collision Fingerprint (DCF) was recently proposed with the goal of producing concise, physically significant representations, generating descriptors via dynamical probing of atomic structures. In this work, we benchmark DCF using a dataset composed of 120 two-dimensional carbon allotropes and compare its performance with the widely considered Matminer library. The analysis employs three regression models, linear regression, decision tree, and XGBoost, evaluated over train and test partitions ranging from 10\% to 90\% and repeated over multiple random seeds in order to characterize statistical variability. The obtained results demonstrate that DCF easily matches Matminer in terms of predicting accuracy across all learning algorithms. However, it accomplishes this using descriptors that are significantly lower dimensional, pointing to manageable computing costs. Moreover, compared to the rather technical Matminer descriptions, the DCF exhibits considerably clearer physical interpretability. These findings suggest that DCF is a significant substitute for high-dimensional descriptor libraries as structural representation since it is both computationally flexible and physically grounded.

Optical emission spectroscopy reveals that, unlike pulsed-DCMS where Ar$^{+}$ ions dominate, HiPIMS discharges are characterised by strong Y$^{+}$ emission, evidencing high yttrium ionisation and substantial self-sputter recycling. The critical working pressure (P$_c$) required to obtain transparent and photochromic films is higher for HiPIMS (Pc $\approx$ 1.0 Pa) than for pulsed-DCMS (Pc $\approx$ 0.5 Pa). Although films deposited near Pc exhibit similar solar transmittance (~72 %) and lattice parameters (5.38--5.39 Å), the pulsed-DCMS film shows a substantially higher relative photochromic contrast (34 %) and a lower optical band gap (2.70 eV) compared with the HiPIMS film (9 % contrast and 2.94 eV). This difference is partly attributed to a lower oxygen-to-hydrogen atomic ratio in the pulsed-DCMS film. Structurally, HiPIMS films are largely polycrystalline with random out-of-plane crystallographic orientation, whereas pulsed-DCMS films exhibit a pronounced <100> out-of-plane preferred orientation. These results demonstrate that, beyond composition, thin-film growth conditions and microstructure play a crucial role in governing the photochromic performance of YHO.

Abstract: Adequate characterization of two-dimensional materials with low energy barriers for impurity adsorption is key for advancing applications based on catalysis, sensing, and surface functionalization. However, first-principles methods, such as DFT, are often computationally extremely expensive for feasible large-scale screenings. Given such a scenario, we address a data-driven approach which integrates the semi-empirical Extended Huckel Method with machine learning techniques to estimate adsorption energy barriers in the case of three relevant chalcogen impurities, S, Se and Te. With this aim, we consider the 4036 2D materials found in the C2DB. The scheme employs the EHM to compute energy profiles along three in-plane migration paths, from which average barriers can be derived. The equilibrium distance between the impurity and the 2D surface is not calculated from a tie-consuming geometry optimization. Instead, it is estimated from a simple effective phenomenological expression. Physicochemical descriptors are then obtained from the Matminer library for curated features. Four different ML models are tested, with the XGBoost leading to the highest performance. We further use SHAP to verify the resulting predictions, focusing on the $\sim1,500$ materials displaying the lowest barrier values. As it could be anticipated, we establish that the average valence electron count, electronegativity, and atomic number are typically the most relevant attributes to validate the ML model. But we also are able to determine, for the different chalcogen atoms, which other few descriptors likewise considerably influence the adsorption properties. Our results show that when combined with interpretable ML protocols, EHM can produce a scalable framework for choosing 2D structures that exhibit the desired capture/release dynamics pertinent in a variety of utilization.

Polarization-resolved SHG and THG measurements exhibit pronounced anisotropy, with emission patterns well-described by theoretical models derived from the khi(2) and khi(3) tensor elements. The material demonstrates exceptionally high nonlinear susceptibilities, with khi(2) ~ 10^(-8) m/V and khi(3) ~ 10^(-17) m^2/V^2 which is a few orders of magnitude greater than comparable 2D materials reported in the literature.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: XPS是研究电池材料化学状态和界面过程的有力技术，但对硅基负极等复杂异质微结构的定量解释存在困难，因为锂化过程会产生强无序Li$_x$Si相和晶态-非晶态转变，这些特征难以表征。

Method: 开发了一个计算框架，结合机器学习预测核心能级结合能与大规模原子模拟（大正则蒙特卡洛GCMC和分子动力学MD，由机器学习势驱动），系统采样锂化状态和局域原子环境。

Result: 该方法生成的化学计量图与实验观测的XPS特征趋势匹配，包括与晶态-非晶态无序化相关的独特Si 2p光谱特征，这种无序化驱动了早期脱锂过程。

Conclusion: 该计算框架能够定量解释硅基负极在电化学循环中的XPS光谱，为理解复杂异质微结构对电池材料性能的影响提供了新工具。

Abstract: X-ray Photoelectron Spectroscopy (XPS) is a powerful technique to probe chemical states and interfacial processes in battery materials, but a quantitative interpretation is often hindered by the complex, heterogeneous microstructures that form during operation and dominate electrochemical cycling. Silicon based anodes represent a paradigmatic example in Li batteries, as (de)lithiation proceeds through the formation of strongly disordered Li$_x$Si phases and crystal-amorphous transformations that are hard to characterize. Here, we introduce a computational framework that combines machine-learning (ML) prediction of core-level binding energies to large-scale atomistic simulations -- Grand Canonical Monte Carlo (GCMC) complemented with molecular dynamics (MD), driven by a ML potential -- for a systematic sampling of lithiation states and local atomic environments. This approach yields stoichiometry maps that match the characteristic experimental trends observed in operando and ex situ XPS measurements, including the distinctive Si $2p$ spectroscopic signatures associated with the crystal-to-amorphous disordering driving early delithiation.

Abstract: Landau level spectroscopy plays an important role in modern condensed-matter physics. In this technique, electrons in a solid are subjected to quantizing magnetic fields and probed experimentally, often through optical methods. Direct and detailed insights into the electronic properties of crystalline materials are obtained, particularly the properties related to their band structure. Landau level spectroscopy enables the precise extraction of key parameters such as effective mass, carrier density, mobility, and band gap, and serves as a powerful tool for studying interactions between electrons and other quasiparticles in solids. Over its more than seventy-year history, Landau level spectroscopy has been applied mainly to semiconductors and semimetals. Today, its scope also includes graphene-based systems, surface and bulk states in topological materials, and other emergent systems with a narrow or vanishing band gap. In this work, we review the fundamentals of Landau level spectroscopy and illustrate them with selected examples from the literature.

### [28] [Accounting for the length-scale dependence of thermal diffusivity in 3C-SiC measured with transient thermal gratings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23247)
*Keshav Vasudeva,Samuel Huberman,Angus P. C. Wylie,Maxwell Rae,Joey Demiane,Jamal A. Haibeh,Elena Botica-Artalejo,Kevin B. Woller,Michael P. Short,Sara E. Ferry*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统泵浦-探针光学方法（如瞬态光栅光谱）在测量声子主导的陶瓷材料时，由于长平均自由程声子在实验尺度上未达到平衡，会低估体热扩散率。需要建立理论指导的实验框架来量化离子辐照损伤对陶瓷热输运性能的降解。

Method: 结合原位瞬态光栅光谱测量与Si4+离子辐照实验（300°C和550°C，0.5-1 dpa），采用密度泛函理论指导的玻尔兹曼输运方程求解，分析晶界密度、温度和缺陷浓度对测量差异的影响。

Result: 揭示了激光闪光分析与瞬态光栅光谱测量热扩散率之间的差异随晶界密度、温度和缺陷浓度的变化规律，提出了无量纲抑制因子来解释这种差异，并验证了该因子能够统一中子辐照与离子辐照3C-SiC的热缺陷电阻测量结果。

Conclusion: 建立了一个理论指导的实验框架，能够定量、原位追踪离子辐照损伤引起的陶瓷热输运性能退化，为核材料等极端环境下陶瓷材料的热性能评估提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Pump-probe optical methods like transient grating spectroscopy (TGS) enable rapid, nondestructive thermoelastic property measurements. But, in phonon-dominated ceramics, they can underpredict bulk thermal diffusivity when long mean free path (MFP) phonons do not equilibrate over experimental length scales. We combine in situ TGS with Si4+ ion irradiation of CVD 3C-SiC (300 and 550C, 0.5-1 dpa) and density functional theory informed Boltzmann transport equation solutions to understand the origins of this offset. We show how the discrepancy between laser flash analysis (LFA) and TGS-measured thermal diffusivity varies with grain-boundary density, temperature, and defect concentration. We introduce a dimensionless suppression factor that accounts for this discrepancy and demonstrate its utility by using it to show an agreement between the thermal defect resistance of neutron irradiated 3C-SiC (measured using LFA) and ion irradiated 3C-SiC (measured using TGS). This theory-informed experimental framework enables quantitative, in situ tracking of ion irradiation damage induced thermal transport degradation in ceramics.

### [32] [The Anyon Zeno Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22322)
*David F. Mross*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在分数量子霍尔干涉实验中检测任意子编织相位时的动力学行为，特别是测量过程如何影响局域任意子的隧穿行为。

Method: 使用嵌入反点的干涉仪，在量子芝诺机制下工作，其中局域任意子的裸隧穿速率远低于测量速率。分析量子芝诺抑制的隧穿速率与编织相位和量子点接触透射率的关系。

Result: 主要预测：干涉仪电导的自相关时间随偏置电流增加而增加。这种效应可用于实验控制任意子动力学，特别是延长局域任意子的寿命。

Conclusion: 在分数量子霍尔干涉实验中检测任意子编织相位会产生量子芝诺效应，导致局域任意子被测量过程困住。这种效应可用于通过偏置电流控制任意子动力学，为实验操控任意子提供了新途径。

Abstract: Two anyons encircling each other acquire a quantized braiding phase that is independent of their spatial separation. We show that detecting this phase in a fractional quantum Hall interference experiment results in a quantum Zeno effect: a localized anyon is trapped by constant observation from a stream of anyons supplied by the measurement current. Interferometers with an embedded antidot are ideal for accessing the Zeno regime, where the bare tunneling rate of localized anyons is much lower than the measurement rate. The Zeno-suppressed tunneling rate of the trapped anyon depends on the braiding phase and the transmission of the quantum point contacts. Our primary prediction is that the autocorrelation time of the conductance through the interferometer increases with the bias current. This effect may be used to experimentally control the anyon dynamics, in particular to increase the lifetime of localized anyons.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索范德华异质结在面内电场作用下的量子干涉现象，为相干量子动力学提供直接可观测的探针，并实现更精确的工程调控和表征。

Result: 识别出两种特征输运信号：1) 带重叠区中周期为1/F的Landau-Zener-Stückelberg振荡，类似于电场诱导的量子振荡；2) 在F∝T₀³/²处的显著共振峰，由层间隧穿强度T₀决定。

Abstract: We demonstrate the presence of quantum interference effects in van der Waals heterostructures subject to in-plane electric fields. The in-plane field $F$ accelerates carriers through a hybridized band edge, and interlayer Zener tunneling occurs by distinct pathways, resulting in a solid-state quantum interferometer with imprints in transport observables. For parabolic-band bilayers, we identify two characteristic signatures which are observable in lateral conductance: Landau-Zener-Stuckelberg oscillations in the band-overlap regime periodic in $1/F$ at small fields, resembling electric-field induced quantum oscillations, and a pronounced resonance at $F\propto T_0^{3/2}$ set by the interlayer tunneling $T_0$. These features provide a directly accessible probe of coherent interferometric dynamics in van der Waals heterostructures, and could be harnessed for more precise engineering and characterization.

### [34] [First-principles and tight-binding analysis of thermoelectricity in irradiated WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22789)

Motivation: 探索光场调控对二维过渡金属硫化物纳米带热电性能的增强机制，旨在通过非平衡驱动实现高效热电转换，为光控热电器件设计提供理论指导。

Method: 采用六轨道紧束缚模型描述电子结构，包含原子自旋轨道耦合；通过Peierls替换引入周期驱动，在高频极限下映射到有效静态Floquet哈密顿量；结合Landauer-Büttiker形式计算相干输运；通过密度泛函微扰理论和声子玻尔兹曼输运方程迭代求解获得晶格热导率。

Result: 光诱导跃迁重整化重塑了费米能级附近的能带色散和透射谱，改变了决定电导、热导和塞贝克系数的Landauer输运积分；结合自旋轨道驱动的能带分裂和增强的非谐散射导致的晶格热导率降低，热电优值ZT在宽温度范围内超过1。

Conclusion: 光场调控与自旋轨道耦合的协同效应可显著增强WSe₂纳米带的热电性能，为实现高效光控热电能量转换提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: Electronic and thermoelectric transport in zigzag monolayer WSe$_2$ nanoribbons are studied under monochromatic irradiation. The electronic structure is described within a six-orbital tight-binding framework constructed from the relevant tungsten and selenium orbitals, with atomic spin-orbit coupling included explicitly. Periodic driving is incorporated via the Peierls substitution, and in the high-frequency limit the system is mapped onto an effective static Floquet Hamiltonian with polarization-dependent renormalized hoppings. Coherent transport is evaluated using wave-function matching within the Landauer-Büttiker formalism. The lattice thermal conductivity is obtained independently from density functional perturbation theory combined with an iterative solution of the phonon Boltzmann transport equation. Light-induced hopping renormalization reshapes the band dispersion and transmission spectrum near the Fermi level, modifying the Landauer transport integrals that determine electrical and thermal conductances and the Seebeck coefficient. Together with spin-orbit-driven band splitting and reduced lattice thermal conductivity from enhanced anharmonic scattering, this leads to a thermoelectric figure of merit $ZT$ exceeding unity over a broad temperature range.

</details>


### [35] [Coupling-energy driven pumping through quantum dots: the role of coherences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23099)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究两种电子泵浦设置：第一种通过开关量子点与引线之间的耦合驱动；第二种通过测量量子点占据数驱动。在无库仑相互作用情况下推导任意强隧穿耦合的精确解。

Result: 识别出具有最优泵浦电流或最优能量效率的参数区域，并讨论了两种泵浦机制之间的相似性。

Conclusion: 非共振隧穿和相干性在量子点电子泵浦中起关键作用，特别是在最低阶隧穿过程被抑制的情况下，仅通过耦合能量调制就能实现有效的电子泵浦。

Abstract: We study the impact of off-resonant tunneling and coherences on the electron pumping through quantum dots. Thereby, we focus on two electron-pump setups where lowest-order tunneling processes are suppressed and the pump is exclusively driven by modulations of the coupling energy. The first setup is driven by switching on and off the couplings between the quantum dot and the leads, while the second setup employs measurements of the dot occupation. We derive exact solutions for arbitrarily strong tunnel couplings in the absence of Coulomb interaction, identify parameter regimes with optimal pumping currents or optimal energy efficiency, and discuss similarities between both pumping mechanisms.

### [36] [Dimensional and doping stability of Peierls charge density waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23208)
*Aitor Garcia-Ruiz,Che-pin Hsu,Ming-Hao Liu,Marcin Mucha-Kruczynski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 研究测试了Peierls不稳定性在有限掺杂和链间杂化下的鲁棒性，发现堆叠几何在远离半填充时对稳定CDW序起决定性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Peierls不稳定性是一维金属链在半填充时自发二聚化的典型CDW形成机制，但对其在有限掺杂和链间杂化条件下的鲁棒性了解有限，需要研究耦合原子链模型中的相图控制因素。

Method: 研究有限厚度相同链阵列中的Peierls不稳定性，分析不同堆叠几何（平行耦合链和斜耦合链）在有限掺杂和链间杂化条件下的行为。

Result: 平行耦合链表现出双稳态区域，其中正常态和二聚化态作为总能量的局部最小值共存；斜耦合链在掺杂时显示重入CDW序。堆叠几何对远离半填充时的CDW序稳定起决定性作用。

Conclusion: 即使是最简单的耦合原子链模型，其相图也受掺杂、晶格刚度和链间耦合几何的丰富控制，堆叠几何在稳定掺杂系统中的CDW序方面起关键作用。

Abstract: The Peierls instability, the spontaneous dimerization of a one-dimensional metallic chain at half filling, is a paradigmatic mechanism for charge-density-wave (CDW) formation. Here we test its robustness under finite doping and interchain hybridization in finite-thickness arrays of identical chains. We find that the stacking geometry plays a decisive role in stabilizing CDW order away from half filling. In particular, parallel-coupled chains exhibit a bistable regime where the normal and dimerized states coexist as local minima of the total energy, while skew-coupled chains display reentrant CDW order upon doping. Our results demonstrate that even minimal models of coupled atomic chains host rich phase diagrams controlled by doping, lattice rigidity, and interchain coupling geometry.

</details>


### [37] [Extrinsic Spin Splitter Currents in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23273)
*Sanjay Sarkar,Sayan Sarkar,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文建立了外禀自旋分裂电流的统一半经典理论，并将其应用于d波交变磁体FeSb2，发现非对称杂质散射是自旋分裂电流的主要通道，且外禀自旋电导率具有时间反演对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体具有动量依赖的自旋分裂但净磁化为零，这使其能够通过外部电场分离相反极化的载流子产生横向自旋电流（自旋分裂效应）。目前需要建立统一的理论框架来理解线性外禀自旋分裂电流的机制。

Method: 发展了线性外禀自旋分裂电流的统一半经典理论，包含了杂质诱导的侧向跳跃和偏斜散射贡献，并将该理论应用于d波交变磁体FeSb2。

Result: 发现非对称杂质散射是自旋分裂电流的主要通道。令人惊讶的是，由此产生的外禀自旋电导率具有时间反演对称性，这与先前研究的对称散射产生的自旋分裂响应不同。

Conclusion: 非对称杂质散射在交变磁体自旋分裂效应中起主导作用，且这种外禀机制产生的自旋电导率具有时间反演对称性，为交变磁体自旋输运提供了新的理论见解。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting despite having zero net magnetization. This enables a spin-splitter effect in which an external electric field generates transverse spin currents by separating oppositely polarized carriers. Here, we develop a unified semiclassical theory of linear extrinsic spin-splitter currents, incorporating impurity-induced side-jump and skew-scattering contributions, and apply it to the $d$-wave altermagnet \ch{FeSb2}. We demonstrate that asymmetric impurity scattering provides a dominant channel for spin-splitter currents. Remarkably, the resulting extrinsic spin conductivity is time-reversal even, in contrast to previously studied spin-splitter responses arising from symmetric scattering.

</details>


### [38] [Electromechanical Switching and Momentum-Selective Transport in Geometry-Defined Blue Phosphorus Homojunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23298)
*Zewen Wu,Min Zhou,Yanxia Xing,Xianghua Kong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 双层蓝磷中通过局部气泡褶皱形成几何定义的金属-半导体-金属同质结，无需化学掺杂或异质界面，实现从弹道输运到隧穿输运的转变，并展示了两种机电器件概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发不依赖化学异质性的本征同质结是未来二维器件发展的关键挑战。传统方法需要化学掺杂或异质界面，而本文探索通过纯几何结构调控实现金属-半导体转变的新途径。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算研究双层蓝磷中局部气泡褶皱的几何结构，通过增大层间分离距离在金属性A₁B₁堆叠双层中打开带隙，形成半导体势垒。结合第一性原理量子输运模拟分析输运机制转变。

Result: 气泡形成导致输运从弹道向隧穿转变，透射率随气泡宽度指数衰减但对高度和凸起方向不敏感。结作为取向依赖的k空间滤波器，产生输运各向异性和动量选择性。轨道分辨散射分析显示层内键合通道在形变下持续而层间杂化通道被淬灭，σ型键合比π型键合具有更高电导。

Conclusion: 几何定义的金属-半导体-金属同质结为二维器件提供了新设计范式，无需化学掺杂即可实现电学功能。基于此提出了两种机电器件概念：机械可开关存储器（ON/OFF比达30）和纳米级滑动变阻器（Å尺度位移传感的指数电阻调谐）。

Abstract: Developing intrinsic homojunctions without chemical heterogeneity remains a key challenge in future two - dimensional devices. Here, we report a geometry - defined metal--semiconductor--metal homojunction in bilayer blue phosphorus (BlueP) created by a localized bubble corrugation, without chemical doping or foreign - material interfaces. First - principles calculations show that enlarging the interlayer separation in the metallic A\(_1\)B\(_1\) - stacked BlueP bilayer opens a band gap, enabling a semiconducting barrier embedded between metallic segments. First - principles quantum - transport simulations reveal a crossover from ballistic to tunneling transport upon bubble formation. In the tunneling regime, transmission decreases exponentially with bubble width while remaining weakly sensitive to bubble height and bulging direction. The junction acts as an orientation - dependent \(k\) - space filter, producing transport anisotropy and momentum selectivity. Orbital - resolved scattering analysis shows that intralayer - bonding channels persist under deformation whereas interlayer - hybridized channels are quenched, and that σ- type bonding yields higher conductance than π- type bonding. These insights motivate two electromechanical device concepts: a mechanically switchable memory element with ON/OFF ratios up to 30 and a nanoscale sliding rheostat with reproducible exponential resistance tuning for Å- scale displacement sensing.

### [39] [Interplay of Gauss Law and the fermion sign problem in quantum link models with dynamical matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22332)
*Pallabi Dey,Debasish Banerjee,Emilie Huffman*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 量子链接模型在特定条件下无符号问题，其基态位于特定高斯定律扇区，可通过meron簇算法有效采样


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究耦合到自旋-1/2 U(1)规范场的量子链接模型，探索其在量子电动力学中预期的库仑相和其他禁闭相的可能性

Method: 使用精确对角化技术分析无磁场模型，证明基态位于特定高斯定律扇区，并开发meron簇算法进行采样

Result: 证明无磁场模型的基态始终位于满足(G_e,G_o)=(d,-d)的扇区，该扇区无费米子符号问题，meron簇算法能有效采样该扇区基态

Conclusion: 量子链接模型在特定高斯定律扇区无符号问题，为研究QED库仑相提供了可行的计算框架，meron簇算法是该问题的有效数值工具

Abstract: Quantum Link Models with dynamical matter coupled to spin-$\frac{1}{2} \ \rm U(1)$ gauge fields in $d=2+1 $ and $3+1$ can potentially give rise to the Coulomb phase expected in quantum electrodynamics (QED) and other confining phases. Using exact diagonalization techniques, we show that the ground state in a class of models without the magnetic field always lies in the sector which satisfies $(G_e,G_o) = (d,\ -d)$, where $d$ is the spatial dimension and $e$ and $o$ are even and odd sites. It can be analytically proven that this sector is free of the fermion sign problem. We also demonstrate that a meron cluster algorithm for the problem naturally samples the ground states of the Hamiltonian in the aforementioned Gauss Law sector.

### [40] [The hadronic tensor from four-point functions on the lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22379)
*Christian Zimmermann,Terrence Draper,Jian Liang,Keh-Fei Liu,Raza Sabbir Sufian,Bigeng Wang*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该论文扩展了格点QCD中核子强子张量的计算，通过使用随机源技术覆盖更广泛的动量转移范围，为结构函数研究提供更全面的数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子张量是计算中微子-核子散射等轻子-强子相互作用截面的核心非微扰对象，通常用结构函数参数化。在格点上计算该矩阵元素需要处理从欧氏时间到闵氏空间的逆问题重构。先前计算受限于动量转移范围，需要扩展到更广泛的运动学区域以研究结构函数。

Method: 采用随机源技术计算四端点函数，能够在广泛的运动学区域内获得所需数据。使用clover费米子系综，参数为：π介子质量223 MeV，格点间距0.085 fm。扩展了先前核子计算中的动量转移范围。

Result: 论文呈现了模拟的概述和一些初步结果。通过使用随机源技术，成功实现了在更广泛动量转移范围内的计算，为结构函数研究提供了更全面的数据基础。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效扩展格点QCD中强子张量的计算范围，为研究中微子-核子散射等过程的非微扰结构函数提供了重要工具。初步结果表明技术路线的可行性，为后续更精确的结构函数计算奠定了基础。

Abstract: The hadronic tensor is the central non-perturbative object in the calculation of the cross section of lepton-hadron interactions like neutrino-nucleon scattering. It is usually parameterized in terms of structure functions, which encode all necessary information for all kinematic regions. Moreover, the structure functions can be factorized in terms of parton distribution functions (PDFs) and contains information on hadron resonances. On the lattice, we can calculate the corresponding matrix element of two quark-bilinear currents with a relative Euclidean time separation. The reconstruction of the hadronic tensor in Minkowski space requires appropriate dealing with the corresponding inverse problem. In our current work, we extend previous calculations on the nucleon by considering a much larger range of momentum transfers, which is inevitable in the context of structure functions. This can be achieved by using stochastic sources, which allows us to calculate the required four-point functions in a broad kinematic region. We employ a clover fermion ensemble at pion mass $m_π= 223~\mathrm{MeV}$ and lattice spacing $a=0.085~\mathrm{fm}$. In these proceedings, we will give an overview of our simulation and present some first preliminary results.

</details>


### [41] [Generalization of lattice Dirac operator index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22858)
*Shoto Aoki,Hajime Fujita,Hidenori Fukaya,Mikio Furuta,Shinichiroh Matsuo,Tetsuya Onogi,Satoshi Yamaguchi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于Ginsparg-Wilson关系的重叠狄拉克算子指标定义存在局限性：仅适用于偶数维平坦环面，无法处理带边界流形、弯曲边界或包含引力背景效应的情况，且难以定义奇偶维度的模2指标。

Method: 采用K理论方法，通过威尔逊狄拉克算子的谱流进行分类，构建了狄拉克算子指标的综合晶格表述。该方法能够处理带边界的Atiyah-Patodi-Singer指标、弯曲边界情况，并自然扩展到奇偶维度的模2指标。

Result: 提出了数学证明并提供了数值证据支持该表述。新方法克服了传统重叠狄拉克算子指标的限制，能够应用于更广泛的几何和拓扑场景，包括带边界流形、弯曲边界和引力背景效应。

Conclusion: 基于K理论和威尔逊狄拉克算子谱流的晶格表述为狄拉克算子指标提供了更通用、更灵活的理论框架，扩展了晶格场论中拓扑指标的应用范围，特别适用于边界问题和奇偶维度的模2指标计算。

Abstract: We provide a comprehensive lattice formulation of various types of the Dirac operator indices, employing $K$-theory to classify the Wilson Dirac operator via its spectral flow. In contrast to the index of the overlap Dirac operator defined through the Ginsparg-Wilson relation, which is restricted to flat tori in even dimensions, our formulation offers several key advantages: 1) It can be applied straightforwardly to the Atiyah-Patodi-Singer index for manifolds with boundary. 2) The boundary can be curved, allowing for the inclusion of gravitational background effects. 3) The mod-2 index in both even and odd dimensions can be defined as a natural extension of the same formulation. In this talk, we present the mathematical proof and provide numerical evidence supporting the formulation.

</details>

Conclusion: 该方法为有效场论中计算ρ介子形状因子提供了可行途径，并规划了格点计算的实现方案，为从头计算方法奠定了基础

Abstract: The calculation of resonance form factors in effective field theory as well as on the lattice is a highly challenging task. In a recent paper, we proposed a novel method based on the introduction of a background field and the Feynman-Hellmann theorem to address the problem, and applied it to a toy model. In the present work we use this method for the electromagnetic form factors of the $ρ$-meson. By matching the results to Chiral Perturbation Theory, we provide a first, crude estimate of all three form factors of the $ρ$-meson within the effective field theory. Contact contributions to these form factors turn out to be substantial. A procedure for lattice calculations is outlined, paving the way for an ab initio approach to the problem.

</details>

Abstract: In this proceeding, we discuss the finite-size scaling analysis of the order parameter related to the chiral phase transition in QCD with two massless quarks. We observe that infinite volume extrapolated data for the order parameter agree reasonably well with the expected $O(2)$ scaling behavior even for physical ratios of the light-to-strange quark mass ratio. We quantify deviations from asymptotic scaling and perform a detailed analysis of the influence of finite-size effects in terms of temperature and quark masses at a fixed lattice cutoff. This is crucial for improving the reliability of the infinite-volume extrapolated estimate of the chiral order parameter and for a more precise determination of chiral phase transition temperature from direct Lattice QCD simulations.

### [47] [Symmetric Mass Generation via Multicriticality in a 3D Lattice Gross-Neveu Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23158)
*Sandip Maiti,Debasish Banerjee,Shailesh Chandrasekharan,Marina K. Marinkovic*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模蒙特卡洛模拟，在三维晶格模型中探索了两种无质量交错费米子通过两个四费米子相互作用耦合的相图，揭示了三种不同相和相变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解费米子质量产生的传统和非传统机制，特别是在具有多个四费米子相互作用的晶格模型中，探索相图结构和相变特性。

Method: 采用大规模费米子袋蒙特卡洛模拟方法，在三维晶格模型中研究两种无质量交错费米子通过两个独立四费米子相互作用(U_I和U_B)耦合的系统。

Result: 在(U_I, U_B)参数空间中识别出三种相：无质量费米子相、对称性破缺大质量相和对称大质量相。当U_B=0时，系统经历从无质量相到对称大质量相的直接连续相变；引入非零U_B后，该直接相变分裂为两个连续相变，中间出现对称性破缺相。无质量相到破缺相的相变属于Gross-Neveu普适类，而破缺相到对称大质量相的相变属于三维XY普适类。

Conclusion: 零耦合处的特殊点作为多临界点组织周围的相结构，为费米子质量产生的传统和非传统机制提供了统一的晶格视角，表明直接相变是更丰富相图结构中的特殊情况。

Abstract: We investigate a three-dimensional lattice model of two flavors of massless staggered fermions coupled through two independent four-fermion interactions, $U_I$ and $U_B$. Using large-scale fermion-bag Monte Carlo simulations, we map out the phase diagram in the $(U_I, U_B)$ parameter space and identify three distinct phases: a massless fermion phase, a symmetry-broken massive phase, and a symmetric massive phase. When one of the interactions is absent ($U_B=0$), the system undergoes a single continuous transition directly connecting the massless and symmetric massive phases, a feature previously associated with unconventional fermion mass generation. We find that turning on a nonzero $U_B$ separates this direct transition into two successive transitions with an intermediate symmetry-broken phase. The transition from the massless to the broken phase belongs to the Gross-Neveu universality class, while the transition from the broken to the symmetric massive phase falls into the three-dimensional XY universality class. Our results indicate that the special point at vanishing coupling, where the direct transition occurs, plays the role of a multicritical point organizing the surrounding phase structure. These findings provide a unified lattice perspective on conventional and unconventional mechanisms of fermion mass generation within a single model.

### [49] [Conformal symmetry in force-free electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22262)
*Huiquan Li,Jianyong Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了闵可夫斯基时空中无力电动力学（FFE）存在共形对称性，揭示了特定自由函数选择下，无力磁层在莫比乌斯变换下的不变性，建立了已知解之间的结构联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无力电动力学是描述天体周围磁层的基础框架，但一般情况下包含源的无力场在保角映射下不能保持物理可容许性。本文旨在探索在特定条件下能否实现共形不变性，从而揭示无力磁层解之间的深层结构关系。

Method: 通过分析无力电动力学的控制方程，特别是流方程，证明其在莫比乌斯变换下的不变性。研究特定自由函数选择下共形对称性的实现条件，并分析这种对称性如何映射不同解之间的区域对应关系。

Result: 证明了无力电动力学的流方程在莫比乌斯变换下具有不变性，这种共形对称性建立了已知解之间的结构联系。特别地，该对称性将一个解的磁层视界（光面）内部区域映射到其对偶解的外部区域，反之亦然。

Conclusion: 无力电动力学在特定条件下具有共形对称性，这一发现不仅为理解无力磁层的数学结构提供了新视角，而且通过莫比乌斯变换建立了不同解之间的对应关系，揭示了磁层视界内外区域的深层联系。

Abstract: It is shown that conformal symmetry exists in force-free electrodynamics (FFE) in Minkowski spacetime, a foundational framework for describing magnetospheres around astronomical objects. In force-free magnetospheres, charges are constrained to move along magnetic field lines and experience zero Lorentz force, due to the everywhere perpendicular orientation of electric and magnetic fields. However, a general angle-preserving conformal mapping of force-free fields does not necessarily produce another physically admissible force-free configuration when sources are present. In this work, we demonstrate that such invariance can nevertheless arise for certain choices of the free functions. Specifically, the governing stream equation is shown to be invariant under Möbius transformations. This symmetry reveals a structural linkage between known solutions and, notably, maps the region inside a magnetospheric horizon (the lightsurface) of one solution to the exterior of its dual counterpart, and vice versa.

</details>

Method: 构建广义Dymnikova黑洞模型，包含完美流体暗物质和弦云；推导Hawking温度和比热容；分析光子动力学（光子球和黑洞阴影）；研究大质量测试粒子运动、圆轨道和稳定性条件；计算准周期振荡的基本星周频率

Abstract: The Dymnikova black hole represents a regular spacetime solution interpolating between a de Sitter core and an asymptotically Schwarzschild geometry. We analyze how these additional matter sources modify the thermodynamic, optical, and dynamical properties of the spacetime.
  We derive the Hawking temperature and specific heat capacity and examine the thermal stability and phase structure of the black hole. The results reveal non-monotonic temperature behavior and parameter-dependent phase transitions. We further study photon dynamics, including the photon sphere and black hole shadow, and show that both PFDM and string cloud parameters significantly affect the shadow radius and strong-field structure.
  Additionally, we investigate the motion of massive test particles, circular orbits, and stability conditions. The corresponding effective potentials, specific energy, and angular momentum are analyzed. Finally, we explore quasi-periodic oscillations (QPOs) by computing the fundamental epicyclic frequencies and discuss how the model parameters encode observable astrophysical signatures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the spacelike Kasner singularity of spherically-symmetric, static and asymptotically flat black holes in Einstein gravity minimally coupled to a massless scalar with a suitable self-interacting scalar potential. We focus on how the asymptotic information such as the mass and scalar charge affect the properties of the Kasner singularity, including the Kasner exponents. We show how a nontrivial integration constant can be extracted from the near-singularity geometry and find a general pattern that this integration constant asymptotes to a linear combination of the mass and scalar charge at large mass limit. We also find that there may be a black hole upper bound on the maximum surviving time of a massive particle inside such a black hole before it falls into the Kasner singularity, and the Schwarzschild black hole saturate this bound.

### [52] [Periodic Analogs of Multiple Black Holes Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22501)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究周期性稳态轴对称多视界解，特别关注具有两个相同等距反向旋转视界的构型，以探索在非零总角动量情况下与静态单视界解的差异，后者在L<4M时无法旋转。

Method: 扩展先前数值研究，构建周期性稳态轴对称多视界解，通过参数化（周期L、质量M、角动量绝对值|J|>0）进行数值分析，特别考察等距和非等距视界配置。

Result: 提供了强数值证据表明存在具有两个相同等距反向旋转视界的周期性稳态轴对称解，且无距离限制；发现等距配置无轴支撑物，而非等距配置会在黑洞间产生支撑物；与静态单视界解形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 成功构建了周期性稳态轴对称多视界解，特别是具有两个相同等距反向旋转视界的构型，这些解在任意距离下都存在且无轴支撑物，为黑洞物理提供了新的解析解。

Abstract: In this article, we extend the numerical studies developed in [arXiv:2210.12898] to construct periodic stationary axisymmetric solutions containing multiple horizons in each fundamental domain. As a direct application, we consider periodic stationary axisymmetric solutions with two identical equidistant counter-rotating horizons. These solutions can be parametrized by the period $L$, the mass $M$, and the absolute value of the angular momentum $|J| >0$. We provide strong numerical evidence for the existence of such configurations, without any restriction in terms of the distance between horizons. This is in sharp contrast with the non-zero total angular momentum case, as it was recently established in \cite{Peraza:2024uto} that static single-horizon periodic solutions cannot be put into rotation if $L < 4M$. It is shown that these solutions do not have any struts on the axis, and it is also explicitly shown that, by taking non-equidistant horizons, struts develop between the black holes. Other global properties of the solutions are also presented.

### [53] [WKB-like approach to the Unruh temperature for arbitrary acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22534)
*Paul M. Alsing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究将Unruh温度从恒定加速度推广到任意时变加速度a(t)的情况，通过隧道效应和WKB方法推导广义Unruh温度公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Unruh温度公式仅适用于恒定加速度情况，而实际物理系统中加速度可能是时变的。需要建立适用于任意加速度a(t)的广义理论框架。

Method: 1. 推广de Gill等人的引力WKB方法；2. 推导适用于任意a(t)的广义Rindler坐标；3. 使用积分加速度χ(t)作为时间坐标；4. 通过隧道效应计算温度；5. 建立与共形坐标的显式变换。

Result: 1. 证明了Schwarzschild-like度规形式不适用于任意a(t)的WKB计算；2. 推导了广义Rindler度规下的Unruh温度公式；3. 给出了多个非平凡a(t)例子的具体温度表达式；4. 建立了恒定加速度小偏离的近似公式；5. 获得了与惯性观测者类似的平面波解结构。

Conclusion: 成功将Unruh效应推广到任意时变加速度情况，建立了完整的理论框架，为研究非稳态加速系统的量子场论效应提供了基础工具。

Abstract: In this work we study the Unruh temperature as arising from tunneling through a barrier for an observer in flat Minkowski spacetime with arbitrary acceleration $a(t)$. For the defining case of constant acceleration $a(t) = a_0$, the Unruh temperature (W. Unruh, Phys. Rev. D 14, 870 (1976)) is given by $k_b\,T_U =\tfrac{\hbar\,a_0}{2\,π\,c}$. Extending the work of de Gill et al. (A. de Gill, D. Singleton, V. Akhmedova and T. Pilling, Am. J. Phys. 78, 685 (2010)) we generalize the gravitational WKB approach to derive the Unruh temperature for arbitrary acceleration. We show that the often employed Schwarzschild-like form of the flat metric is not appropriate for the WKB calculation with an arbitrary $a(t)$, and instead derive a generalized Unruh temperature for the generalized Rindler metric where $a_0\to a(t)$. We derive a generalization of the Rindler coordinates appropriate for arbitrary $a(t)$, and stress the importance of the role of the integrated acceleration $χ(t) = \int^t dt'\,a(t')$, which can also act as a temporal coordinate. We explore several non-trivial examples of $a(t)$ and their generalized Unruh temperatures. We additionally develop an approximation to the Unruh temperature for small deviations away from constant acceleration by the standard approach of considering the negative frequency content of a purely positive frequency plane wave of an inertial observer, as measured by the co-moving arbitrarily accelerated observer. Lastly, we develop and explicit coordinate transformation between the arbitrarily accelerated observer and conformal coordinates, where the plane wave structure of the solutions of the wave equation is readily transparent, and analogous to the form for the inertial observer.

</details>


### [54] [Quantum corrected thermodynamics and horizon quantization of the Reissner--Nordström black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22559)
*S. Jalalzadeh,H. Moradpour*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文为Reissner-Nordström黑洞建立了一个统一的半经典框架，基于Misner-Sharp-Hernandez质量，将准局部视界能量作为热力学变量，推导出量子修正的温度和熵，并通过几何变形因子编码这些修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Reissner-Nordström黑洞建立一个统一的半经典框架，将热力学和量子化整合在Misner-Sharp-Hernandez质量基础上，研究量子修正对黑洞热力学和几何的影响。

Method: 使用Misner-Sharp-Hernandez质量作为基础，将准局部视界能量作为热力学变量，建立逐视界的第一定律和Smarr关系；通过约化相空间量子化获得离散的MSH质量谱；通过简单的乘法因子将量子修正编码到几何变形中。

Result: 获得了离散的MSH质量谱，重现了最小熵间距；量子跃迁产生普朗克尺度的霍金温度修正和熵的对数贡献；量子变形的RN几何保持经典视界位置但修正表面引力；有效应力张量表现为守恒的真空极化源；变形略微降低两个视界温度，减弱内视界不稳定性，并引起光子球和阴影观测量的微小偏移。

Conclusion: 该研究为RN黑洞提供了一个统一的半经典框架，将热力学和量子化整合，量子修正通过简单的几何变形因子编码，为黑洞量子引力效应提供了紧凑的表示，并预测了可观测的微小效应。

Abstract: In this letter, we develop a unified semiclassical framework for the thermodynamics and quantization of the Reissner--Nordström (RN) black hole (BH) based on the Misner--Sharp--Hernandez (MSH) mass. Treating the quasi-local horizon energies as the relevant thermodynamic variables, we formulate a horizon-by-horizon first law and Smarr relation. Using a reduced phase-space quantization, we obtain a discrete MSH mass spectrum for both horizons, which reproduces the minimal entropy spacing. Quantum transitions between adjacent levels yield Planck-scale corrections to the Hawking temperatures and a universal logarithmic contribution to the entropy, consistent with independent approaches to quantum gravity. We encode these corrections into a quantum-deformed RN geometry via a simple multiplicative factor that preserves the classical horizon positions while reproducing the corrected surface gravities. The associated effective stress tensor behaves as a conserved vacuum-polarization source with characteristic $r^{-4}$ falloff and a small trace, providing a compact representation of semiclassical backreaction. The deformation slightly lowers both horizon temperatures, weakens the inner-horizon instability, and induces tiny shifts in photon-sphere and shadow observables for macroscopic BHs.

### [55] [Lorentzian Vacuum Transitions in $f(R)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22561)
*H. García-Compeán,J. Hernández-Aguilar,D. Mata-Pacheco,C. Ramírez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在f(R)引力理论框架下研究标量场势能两个极小值之间的洛伦兹真空跃迁概率，将Wheeler-DeWitt方程的WKB展开推广到修正引力理论


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将之前爱因斯坦引力中的真空跃迁概率研究扩展到f(R)修正引力理论，探索量子引力效应在修正引力理论中的表现

Method: 将Wheeler-DeWitt方程的WKB展开推广到f(R)引力理论至二阶，应用于均匀各向同性FLRW宇宙（零曲率和正曲率），对平直情况在常数Ricci标量假设下获得解析解，对幂律f(R)=R^{1+n}模型获得无此假设的显式解

Result: 平直情况在常数Ricci标量假设下获得任意模型的解析跃迁概率表达式；对幂律模型获得无此假设的显式解；正曲率情况下常数Ricci标量假设不一致，但在近似区域获得解析解；所有情况下都保持爱因斯坦引力中发现的概率一般行为，包括量子修正预测的非奇异初始状态

Conclusion: f(R)引力理论中的真空跃迁概率保持了爱因斯坦引力中的一般特征，但具体概率值以模型依赖的方式增减，量子修正仍预测非奇异初始状态，为修正引力理论中的量子宇宙学提供了新见解

Abstract: We study Lorentzian vacuum transition probabilities between two minima of a scalar field potential within the framework of $f(R)$ gravity. The analysis extends the previously considered WKB expansion of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation to modified gravity theories, up to second order. We apply the general method for homogeneous and isotropic FLRW universes, with zero and positive spatial curvature, for any $f(R)$ model. For the flat case we obtain analytic expressions for the transition probabilities for any model if we assume a constant Ricci scalar; this assumption has been considered in previous studies, in the Euclidean approach, from symmetry arguments. On the other hand, we also obtain explicit solutions without this assumption for power-law $f(R)=R^{1+n}$ models. Moreover, in the positive curvature scenario, we obtain that the assumption of a constant Ricci scalar is not consistent, but we are able to find analytical solutions in approximated regimes. In all cases we have found that the general behavior of the probabilities already found for Einstein Gravity is preserved, including the prediction of a non-singular initial state due to quantum corrections, even though the probabilities increase or decrease in a model dependent way.

Conclusion: 研究证明了在F(R)-Euler-Heisenberg黑洞中，弱引力猜想和弱宇宙监督猜想可以同时兼容，Euler-Heisenberg耦合在裸奇点区域恢复了光子球结构。热力学分析表明小黑洞相是符合WGC的可达热力学状态，为理解量子引力与经典引力之间的相互作用提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay of the Weak Gravity Conjecture (WGC) and the Weak Cosmic Censorship Conjecture (WCCC) in $F(R)$-Euler-Heisenberg black holes in Anti-de Sitter and de Sitter backgrounds. The solution is characterized by the electric charge $q$, the $F(R)$ deviation $f_{R_0}$, the Euler--Heisenberg coupling $λ$, and the constant scalar curvature $R_0$. We establish a universal entropy--extremality relation that provides thermodynamic evidence for the WGC independently of $f_{R_0}$ and $R_0$. Photon sphere analysis from both geodesic and topological perspectives confirms the simultaneous compatibility of the WGC and WCCC, with the Euler--Heisenberg coupling restoring photon spheres in the naked singularity regime. Gravitational lensing in the strong- and weak-deflection limits reveals that the photon sphere radius is independent of the cosmological background while the critical impact parameter nearly doubles in de Sitter. Black hole shadow images under isotropic accretion are constructed. Within the Barrow entropy framework, we uncover van der Waals-type phase transitions and analyze Joule-Thomson expansion, identifying the small black hole phase as the WGC-compatible thermodynamic regime accessible via isenthalpic cooling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 边界条件（分支振幅）和退相干（经典分支选择）在经典宇宙时空涌现中扮演不同角色。环境诱导纠缠产生了涌现的宇宙时间箭头，澄清了量子宇宙学中经典性出现的机制。

Abstract: We analyze the emergence of classical cosmological spacetimes in quantum cosmology by computing the reduced density matrix for long-wavelength curvature perturbations. Starting from standard Hartle--Hawking and tunneling boundary conditions, we emphasize that semiclassical WKB structure and inflationary squeezing do not by themselves yield classicality. Tracing over unobserved degrees of freedom and using the influence functional formalism, we derive the decoherence functional for superhorizon curvature modes during inflation. For a light massive environmental scalar field in the Bunch--Davies vacuum, we obtain an explicit noise kernel and show how a nonzero mass regulates the infrared behavior. We then evaluate decoherence under horizon-based and EFT-motivated coarse grainings, finding efficient suppression of interference between macroscopically distinct perturbation histories in both cases. The analysis clarifies the distinct roles of boundary conditions (branch amplitudes) and decoherence (classical branch selection) and yields an emergent cosmological arrow of time through environment-induced entanglement.
